[30;1m38 | [0m[35mIn normal usage, ``pre-commit`` will trigger with every ``git commit``[0m
[30;1m39 | [0m[35mand every ``git push``. The hooks that trigger in each stage can be[0m
[30;1m40 | [0m[35mconfigured by editing the ``.pre-commit-config.yaml`` file. The files[0m
[30;1m41 | [0m[35mthat have changed will be passed to the various hooks before the git[0m
[30;1m42 | [0m[35moperation completes. If one of the hooks exits with a non-zero[0m
[30;1m43 | [0m[35mexit-code, then the commit (or push) will fail.[0m
[30;1m44 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m45 | [0m[35mManual Usage[0m
